    <h1 class="u-h">
     News, sport and opinion from the Guardian's US edition
    </h1>
    <section aria-expanded="true" class="fc-container fc-container--first fc-container--thrasher flashing-image js-container--first " data-component="palette-styles-new-do-not-delete" data-id="7c0f56e8-d4c4-408f-ba58-c29508c8cf5e" data-link-name="container-1 | palette-styles-new-do-not-delete" id="palette-styles-new-do-not-delete">

        </h2>

      <div class="fc-container--rolled-up-hide fc-container__body" data-id="7c0f56e8-d4c4-408f-ba58-c29508c8cf5e" data-title="Palette styles new do not delete">
       <div class="fc-slice-wrapper">
        <ul class="u-unstyled l-row l-row--cols-1 fc-slice fc-slice--mf">
